## Callbacks

These functions are called by the engine automatically:

| Callback | Description |
|----------|-------------|
| `luna.load()` | Called once after the script is loaded |
| `luna.update(dt)` | Called every frame; `dt` is elapsed seconds |
| `luna.draw()` | Called every frame for rendering |
| `luna.keypressed(key)` | Called when a keyboard key is pressed |
| `luna.keyreleased(key)` | Called when a keyboard key is released |
| `luna.mousepressed(x, y, button)` | Called when a mouse button is pressed |
| `luna.mousereleased(x, y, button)` | Called when a mouse button is released |
| `luna.touchpressed(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch start |
| `luna.touchmoved(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch move |
| `luna.touchreleased(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch end |
| `luna.resize(w, h)` | Called when window is resized |
| `luna.focus(focused)` | Called when window gains/loses focus |
| `luna.quit()` | Called when the window is closed |
| `luna.gamepadpressed(id, button)` | Called on gamepad button press |
| `luna.gamepadreleased(id, button)` | Called on gamepad button release |
| `luna.gamepadaxis(id, axis, value)` | Called on gamepad axis change |

#### `luna.graphics.ensureGlyph`

Ensures a glyph is rasterized and present in the atlas cache.

If the character has already been rasterized, this is a no-op. Otherwise the glyph is rasterized via fontdue and packed into the atlas. @param ch : The

#### `luna.physics.addFrictionJoint`

#### `luna.physics.destroyBody`

Removes a body from the world by disabling it in rapier.

The body slot is kept to preserve stable IDs. The body is set to Static and its rapier rigid body is disabled. @param id : Body

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L900)*

#### `luna.physics.destroyJoint`

Removes a joint from the world. After this call the associated key is invalid and must not be reused.

@param joint_id : Joint

#### `luna.physics.getBodyMut`

Returns a mutable reference to body `id`, or `None` if out of range.

Shape, restitution, layer, mask, velocity, and position mutations are flushed into the rapier simulation on the next `step()` call. @param id : Body

*(undocumented)*

---

#### `luna.physics.setSleepingAllowed`

Sets whether sleeping is allowed for a body.

When sleeping is allowed, the physics engine can deactivate stationary bodies to save CPU. When disabled, the body stays awake indefinitely. @param id : Body @param allowed : true

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L899)*

---

#### `luna.physics.step`

*(undocumented)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L882)*

---

#### `luna.physics.step`

Advances the simulation by `dt` seconds.

1. Rebuild rapier colliders for bodies with changed shape/properties. 2. Push all body positions/velocities into rapier. 3. Step the rapier pipeline. 4. Read back positions/velocities for Dynamic bodies. 5. Record collision events. @param dt : Time

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L882)*

---

#### `luna.event.wait`

Blocks until an event is available or `timeout_ms` milliseconds elapse.

If the queue already contains an event it is returned immediately without sleeping. With a `Some(0)` timeout the queue is polled once and the function returns. @param timeout_ms : integer? @return Event?

*Source: [src/lua_api/event_api.rs](src/lua_api/event_api.rs#L171)*

#### `luna.ai.calculate`

Parses a Lua string into a `FormationType`. Unrecognised strings

default to `FormationType::None`.

@param s : str @return Self Parses from Lua string. Returns an error if the source data is malformed or missing. Computes the 2D steering force for this behavior given the agent's current kinematic state. The force should be added to the agent's velocity (after weighting and truncation by the SteeringManager). For Pursue, Evade, and Flock, this returns `(0.0, 0.0)` because those behaviors need access to other agents' states, which is handled at the AIWorld level. @param agent_pos : (f32, f32) @param agent_vel : (f32, f32) @param max_speed : number @param _dt : number @return Force

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L584)*

#### `luna.ai.learn`

Performs one Bellman Q-learning update.

Updates the Q-value for (`state`, `action`) using the observed `reward` and the estimated value of `next_state`: `Q(s,a) ŌåÉ Q(s,a) + ╬▒[r + ╬│ max_a' Q(s',a') - Q(s,a)]` Silently no-ops if any index is out of range. @param state : integer @param action : integer @param reward : number @param next_state : integer

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L579)*

Accepted strings: `"fsm"`, `"bt"`, `"steering"`, `"fsm+steering"`, `"bt+steering"`. Returns `None` for unrecognized input, allowing the Lua binding to emit a descriptive error rather than silently defaulting. @param s : str @return Self?

#### `luna.ai.setNumber`

Converts a Lua status string into a `BTStatus`.

Accepts `"success"` and `"failure"` literally; any other string (including `"running"`) maps to `Running`. This permissive default ensures that a Lua callback returning an unrecognized string keeps the behavior alive rather than silently succeeding or failing. @param s : str @return Self Parses a Lua string (`"requireOne"` or `"requireAll"`) into a policy. Defaults to `RequireOne` for unrecognized strings. Sets a number value in the local store. @param key : str @param value : number

#### `luna.data.getPackedSize`

Computes the total byte size that `pack` would produce for the given format and values.

For fixed-width types (`b`/`B`/`h`/`H`/`i`/`I`/`l`/`L`/`f`/`d`/`n`) the values are not accessed, so an empty slice may be passed. String types (`s`/`z`) require the corresponding `PackValue::Str` entry to compute the size. @param format : str @param values : [PackValue] @return Result<usize

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L371)*

---

#### `luna.data.pack`

Packs values according to a format string into a `ByteData` buffer.

Format characters: - `<` ŌĆö switch to little-endian (default) - `>` ŌĆö switch to big-endian - `b`/`B` ŌĆö i8 / u8 - `h`/`H` ŌĆö i16 / u16 - `i`/`I` ŌĆö i32 / u32 - `l`/`L` ŌĆö i64 / u64 - `f` ŌĆö f32 - `d`/`n` ŌĆö f64 - `s` ŌĆö length-prefixed string (u32 len + bytes) - `z` ŌĆö null-terminated string - `x` ŌĆö padding byte (zero) @param format : str @param values : [PackValue] @return Result<ByteData

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L369)*

@param node_type : str @param capacity : integer @return integer Remove a node and all connected edges. Items at the node become `Unplaced`. Returns `true` if the node existed. @param node_id : integer @return boolean Add a directed edge between two existing nodes. Returns the edge ID. @param from : integer @param to : integer @param edge_type : str? @return Result<u64 Remove an edge. Items in transit on it become `Unplaced`. #### `luna.automation.load`

*(undocumented)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L272)*

---

#### `luna.automation.load`

Load a script into the simulator, replacing any script with the same name.

The script is indexed by [`Script::name`]. If a script with that name is already registered it is silently overwritten. The active script, if running, is unaffected unless the new script replaces it ŌĆö in that case the replacement takes effect at the next [`Simulator::update`]. @param script : Script

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L272)*

---

#### `luna.automation.parseAction`

*(undocumented)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L276)*

---

#### `luna.automation.parseAction`

Parse an action string into the corresponding variant.

Accepts lowercase strings matching the Lua API convention: `"keypress"`, `"keyrelease"`, `"mousemove"`, `"mousepress"`, `"mouserelease"`, `"mousewheel"`, `"textinput"`, `"wait"`. Returns `None` for any unrecognised string. The match is case-sensitive; `"KeyPress"` and `"KEYPRESS"` are not accepted. @param s : str @return Action?

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L276)*

---

#### `luna.automation.start`

*(undocumented)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L274)*

---

#### `luna.automation.start`

Start playback of the named script from the beginning.

Resets `elapsed` to `0.0` and `next_step_idx` to `0`, then transitions to `Running`. Calling `start` while already running or paused restarts the same or a different script from scratch. Returns `Err` if the script name is not registered. @param name : str @return Result<()

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L274)*

---

#### `luna.automation.unload`

*(undocumented)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L273)*

---

#### `luna.automation.unload`

Remove a loaded script by name.

Returns `true` if the script was found and removed, `false` if no script with that name was loaded. If the removed script is currently active, [`Simulator::stop`] is called automatically, resetting playback to `Idle`. @param name : str @return boolean

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L273)*

---

#### `luna.automation.update`

*(undocumented)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L275)*

---

#### `luna.automation.update`

Advance the playback clock by `dt` seconds and dispatch all due steps.

Adds `dt` to `elapsed` and dispatches every step whose `time <= elapsed` that has not yet fired. Each dispatched step fires at most once. When the last step is dispatched, the simulator transitions to `Complete`. Multiple steps may fire in a single `update` call if `dt` spans several step times. Is a no-op when `state != Running`. @param dt : number @param event_queue : mut EventQueue

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L275)*

---

#### `luna.automation.withDescription`

*(undocumented)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L271)*

---

#### `luna.automation.withDescription`

Create a script with an explicit description string.

Behaves identically to [`Script::new`] but additionally sets the `description` field. Useful when constructing scripts in Rust code that should carry human-readable metadata. @param name : impl Into<String> @param description : impl Into<String> @param steps : table @return Script

*Source: [src/lua_api/automation_api.rs](src/lua_api/automation_api.rs#L271)*

---

#### `luna.raycaster.computeLighting`

Computes ambient + point-light illumination at a world position.

Each light contributes based on inverse-distance falloff within its radius. The result is the sum of ambient light and all point-light contributions, clamped per-channel to [0, 1]. @param x : number @param y : number @param ambient : number @param lights : [PointLight]

*Source: [src/lua_api/raycaster_api.rs](src/lua_api/raycaster_api.rs#L558)*

---
